- DONE this slice: closed a bounded live AI frontend orchestration slice while keeping accounting deferred to phase 2. Focused AI frontend tests, active webclient bootstrap tests, frontend typecheck/build/full tests, focused AI HTTP/runtime/addon/mail tests, and full `make ci` passed. Remaining deferred gaps: deeper AI frontend/discuss orchestration, broader exact UI pixel parity, and accounting remains phase 2.

- DONE this slice: added bounded AI provider retry policy while keeping accounting deferred to phase 2. OpenAI-compatible and Gemini-compatible chat calls now honor `ChatRequest.MaxRetries`; embedding calls now support `EmbeddingRequest.MaxRetries`; retries are capped at 5 and only apply to transient provider failures: HTTP 429, HTTP 5xx, or transport errors. HTTP 400-style provider errors are not retried and provider error bodies/secrets remain hidden. Added regressions for transient chat retry, embedding rate-limit retry, and no retry on bad request. Focused provider, AI, RAG/source, and runtime AI tests passed. Clean exact-patch `make ci` passed.

## Web And Themes

- Expand `owl-compat` with Odoo runtime APIs: `App`, `mount`, lifecycle hooks, `EventBus`, `reactive`, env inheritance, refs, effects, and external listeners.

- Audit finding: OWL compat still lacks Odoo 19 runtime APIs including `OwlError`, component context/status, `useComponent`, refs, destroy/error hooks, `markRaw`, `toRaw`, and scheduler-compatible reactivity.
- Audit finding: QWeb compiler still needs sandboxed expression evaluation plus `t-inherit`, XPath mutation, `t-component`, `t-props`, `t-ref`, slots, `t-on`, and `t-key` validation.
- Audit finding: webclient still needs Odoo-style registry categories/sequences/update events, `makeEnv`, `startServices`, router bus, action/menu/title/ui/rpc/orm service skeletons.
- Audit finding: assets still need manifest sequence splitting, recursive includes, glob resolution, target ops, debug/min hash manifests, XML template registration, and CSS RTL/autoprefix hooks.
- Audit finding: enterprise theme still needs color-scheme service, home-menu action/service, navbar replacement contract, and dark/light variable layers.
